+00003210: 0a3c 703e 2323 2044 6570 6c6f 7969 6e67  .<p>## Deploying
+00003220: 2077 6974 6820 7069 703c 2f70 3e0a 3c70   with pip</p>.<p
+00003230: 3e57 6520 7573 6564 205b 6f64 6f6f 2073  >We used [odoo s
+00003240: 6574 7570 2074 6f6f 6c73 5d28 3c61 2063  etup tools](<a c
+00003250: 6c61 7373 3d22 7265 6665 7265 6e63 6520  lass="reference

+00003290: 6f6c 732d 6f64 6f6f 2f23 7061 636b 6167  ols-odoo/#packag

+000032f0: 2d61 6464 6f6e 3c2f 613e 2920 746f 2067  -addon</a>) to g
+00003300: 656e 6572 6174 6520 7468 6520 7079 7069  enerate the pypi
+00003310: 2066 696c 6573 2066 726f 6d20 7468 6520   files from the 
+00003320: 6f64 6f6f 206d 616e 6966 6573 7473 2e20  odoo manifests. 
+00003330: 546f 2064 6570 6c6f 7920 616e 7920 7061  To deploy any pa
+00003340: 636b 6167 6564 206d 6f64 756c 652c 2073  ckaged module, s
+00003350: 6f20 7468 6174 206f 646f 6f20 6361 6e20  o that odoo can 
+00003360: 6c61 7465 7220 696e 7374 616c 6c20 7468  later install th
+00003370: 656d 2c0a 796f 7520 6361 6e20 6372 6561  em,.you can crea
+00003380: 7465 2061 2076 656e 7620 7769 7468 2074  te a venv with t
+00003390: 6869 7320 6e61 6d65 2028 6974 e280 9973  his name (it...s
+000033a0: 2067 6974 2d69 676e 6f72 6564 290a 3c74   git-ignored).<t
+000033b0: 7420 636c 6173 733d 2264 6f63 7574 696c  t class="docutil
+000033c0: 7320 6c69 7465 7261 6c22 3e60 7368 656c  s literal">`shel
+000033d0: 6c0a 7079 7468 6f6e 203c 7370 616e 2063  l.python <span c

+000033f0: 7061 6e3e 2076 656e 7620 7665 6e76 0a60  pan> venv venv.`
+00003400: 3c2f 7474 3e0a 416e 6420 7468 656e 2070  </tt>.And then p
+00003410: 6970 2d69 6e73 7461 6c6c 2074 6865 6d20  ip-install them

+00003490: 3c2f 613e 292e 3c2f 703e 0a3c 703e 2323  </a>).</p>.<p>##
+000034a0: 2320 4578 616d 706c 653c 2f70 3e0a 3c70  # Example</p>.<p
+000034b0: 3e46 6f72 2069 6e73 7461 6e63 652c 2066  >For instance, f
